    2153             : /** \brief Identify the CRS with reference CRSs.
    2154             :  *
    2155             :  * The candidate CRSs are either hard-coded, or looked in the database when
    2156             :  * it is available.
    2157             :  *
    2158             :  * The method returns a list of matching reference CRS, and the percentage
    2159             :  * (0-100) of confidence in the match. The list is sorted by decreasing
    2160             :  * confidence.
    2161             :  * <ul>
    2162             :  * <li>100% means that the name of the reference entry
    2163             :  * perfectly matches the CRS name, and both are equivalent. In which case a
    2164             :  * single result is returned.
    2165             :  * Note: in the case of a GeographicCRS whose axis
    2166             :  * order is implicit in the input definition (for example ESRI WKT), then axis
    2167             :  * order is ignored for the purpose of identification. That is the CRS built
    2168             :  * from
    2169             :  * GEOGCS["GCS_WGS_1984",DATUM["D_WGS_1984",SPHEROID["WGS_1984",6378137.0,298.257223563]],
    2170             :  * PRIMEM["Greenwich",0.0],UNIT["Degree",0.0174532925199433]]
    2171             :  * will be identified to EPSG:4326, but will not pass a
    2172             :  * isEquivalentTo(EPSG_4326, util::IComparable::Criterion::EQUIVALENT) test,
    2173             :  * but rather isEquivalentTo(EPSG_4326,
    2174             :  * util::IComparable::Criterion::EQUIVALENT_EXCEPT_AXIS_ORDER_GEOGCRS)
    2175             :  * </li>
    2176             :  * <li>90% means that CRS are equivalent, but the names are not exactly the
    2177             :  * same.</li>
    2178             :  * <li>70% means that CRS are equivalent), but the names do not match at
    2179             :  * all.</li>
    2180             :  * <li>25% means that the CRS are not equivalent, but there is some similarity
    2181             :  * in
    2182             :  * the names.</li>
    2183             :  * </ul>
    2184             :  * Other confidence values may be returned by some specialized implementations.
    2185             :  *
    2186             :  * This is implemented for GeodeticCRS, ProjectedCRS, VerticalCRS and
    2187             :  * CompoundCRS.
    2188             :  *
    2189             :  * @param ctx PROJ context, or NULL for default context
    2190             :  * @param obj Object of type CRS. Must not be NULL
    2191             :  * @param auth_name Authority name, or NULL for all authorities
    2192             :  * @param options Placeholder for future options. Should be set to NULL.
    2193             :  * @param out_confidence Output parameter. Pointer to an array of integers that
    2194             :  * will be allocated by the function and filled with the confidence values
    2195             :  * (0-100). There are as many elements in this array as
    2196             :  * proj_list_get_count()
    2197             :  * returns on the return value of this function. *confidence should be
    2198             :  * released with proj_int_list_destroy().
    2199             :  * @return a list of matching reference CRS, or nullptr in case of error.
    2200             :  */
